< review>
First - Jim the manager is the greatest.

Second -  I rented lockers and was broken into when it was under previous ownership.  Now that ExtraSpace has taken over the facility, the security is much better.

Third - Jim the manager is the greatest!

Fourth - March 2017 - Returned from my trip and needed an extra locker.  Jim was very helpful.

Fifth - Did I mention that Jim the manager is the greatest?

it is now almost November 2017 and right after a rate increase I got a letter saying there would be yet another dollar increase for new insurance.  So now the rate increase is 12%.  Ridiculous!  So I complained to Jim about it - he is fun to mess with!  Anyway, he put in for a manager's discount and got it, but told me to expect another rate increase in 6 months. < Review>
So....I used to rent at this location when it was StoreQuest, and my experience there was horrible, so needless to say, I left.  However, as time went on, I found myself needing a storage unit again, and I noticed that what once was StoreQuest had changed to Extra Space Storage.  Because of the change in name, my wife and I decided to drop by and see if anything had actually changed with the way the place was managed.  We spoke with the manager, Jim,  and he kindly took us around and showed us a couple units, and shared with us all of the changes that had taken place since it had been taken over -- things like some of the updated/upgraded security features, tenant rule changes, as well as some of the upgrades to the facility itself.

After visiting and speaking with Jim, we were more than satisfied that this was the place to rent our storage unit.  The facility is super clean, super safe, and the management an staff are great and helpful people.  I would definitely recommend this place over any other public storage places in town.< /Review>

<userid>112752304819815563031<//userid>< review>
A neighborhood park situated in the West Valley, next to Warner Center business district. It includes a children's playground, amphitheatre, plenty of beautiful trees to shade oneself, and a quiet place to do yoga, walk or meditate. This park was here way before the area was built. Right now, it has summer concerts and outdoor movie nights up until September. A great place to relax and enjoy its tranquility.</review>

< review>
People see what they want to see. This park has gone downhill the last two years dramatically. Lots of more drug paraphernalia around the south side of the park., and the grass seems to get Browner.

Bring a blanket with you! Trust me!

During the day the park is fine, the weekends are okay during the day as well. You can bring your kids here and throw a frisbee, play soccer or whatever.

Night time is a whole different story. Especially after 10 or 11 p.m. there are definitely some shady characters sitting at the tables, and parked in their cars.</review>
